## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3d82-1119">Atributos do Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3d82-1119">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d3d82-1120">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3d82-1120">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
